href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>Caroline Sullivan of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> wrote Williams is \xe2\x80\x9ca perfect meeting of ego, self-deprecation and hits\xe2\x80\x9d, adding \xe2\x80\x9cthere really is nobody else, in pop music anyway, who combines monumental hamminess and bone-deep vulnerability quite so effectively.\xe2\x80\x9d<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> \n</p><p>He has been presented many awards, including a record eighteen <a href="/wiki/Brit_Awards" title="Brit Awards">Brit Awards</a>\xe2\x80\x94Best British Male four times, and two awards for Outstanding Contribution to Music and the 2017 Brits Icon for his "lasting impact on <a href="/wiki/British_culture" class="mw-redirect" title="British culture">British culture</a>", and eight German <a href="/wiki/ECHO_(music_award)" class="mw-redirect" title="ECHO (music award)">ECHO</a> awards.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Brits_Winners_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Brits_Winners-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-rhein-zeitung.de_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rhein-zeitung.de-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> In 2004, he was inducted into the <a href="/wiki/UK_Music_Hall_of_Fame" title="UK Music Hall of Fame">UK Music Hall of Fame</a>, after being voted as the Greatest artist of the 1990s.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> He appeared in the 2009 edition of the <i>Guinness Book of World Records</i> when his sell-out show at the BBC Electric Proms at London\'s Roundhouse was screened by more than 250 cinemas across 23 countries to set a new record for the most simultaneous cinematic screenings of a live concert.<sup id="cite_ref-\xe2\x80\x9cGuinness\xe2\x80\x9d_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-\xe2\x80\x9cGuinness\xe2\x80\x9d-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> Williams appears in the list of the all-time Top 100 biggest selling albums in the UK six times\xe2\x80\x93with <a href="/wiki/List_of_best-selling_albums_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="List of best-selling albums in the United Kingdom">four albums in the top 60</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-timesonline.co.uk_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-timesonline.co.uk-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2005, the British public voted \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="/wiki/Angels_(Robbie_Williams_song)" title="Angels (Robbie Williams song)">Angels</a>\xe2\x80\x9d the song they would most like played at their funeral.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> In October 2009, it was announced that he would receive the Outstanding Contribution to British Music award at the <a href="/wiki/2010_Brit_Awards" title="2010 Brit Awards">2010 Brit Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> In September 2010, Williams switched on the <a href="/wiki/Blackpool_illuminations" class="mw-redirect" title="Blackpool illuminations">Blackpool illuminations</a>, stating that it was one of the greatest honours he had achieved.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> In October, <a href="/wiki/Media_Control" class="mw-redirect" title="Media Control">Media Control</a> named Williams the most successful album-artist of the millennium due to the fact that he had spent No. 1 on the <a href="/wiki/German_Albums_Chart" class="mw-redirect" title="German Albums Chart">German Albums Chart</a> for 38 weeks since 2000. He also reached that chart\'s Top Ten 135 times.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>\n<p>Since 2006, Williams has spent most of his time in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> Williams moved back to the UK in 2009 when he bought an <a href="/wiki/Pound_sterling" title="Pound sterling">\xc2\xa3</a>8.5&#160;million mansion in <a href="/wiki/Compton_Bassett" title="Compton Bassett">Compton Bassett</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wiltshire" title="Wiltshire">Wiltshire</a>, nearby to close friend <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Wilkes" title="Jonathan Wilkes">Jonathan Wilkes</a> who lives in <a href="/wiki/Swindon" title="Swindon">Swindon</a>. Williams sold the mansion a year later to move back to Los Angeles. In 2017 he sold his mansion in Beverly Hills for $9.9 million to <a href="/wiki/DJ_Khaled" title="DJ Khaled">DJ Khaled</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> In 2016 he moved into a \xc2\xa317 million mansion in <a href="/wiki/Kensington" title="Kensington">Kensington</a>, West London.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> His next door neighbour in London is <a href="/wiki/Led_Zeppelin" title="Led Zeppelin">Led Zeppelin</a> guitarist <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Page" title="Jimmy Page">Jimmy Page</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Page_126-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Page-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> In a long-running planning battle between the two musicians Page delayed Williams\' plans for an underground swimming pool in 2018, stating construction work would damage his listed mansion, Tower House.<sup id="cite_ref-Page_126-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Page-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Health_issues">Health issues</span></h3>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:27%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x9cTwo of his biggest hits, \xe2\x80\x98<a href="/wiki/Come_Undone_(Robbie_Williams_song)" title="Come Undone (Robbie Williams song)">Come Undone</a>\xe2\x80\x99 and \xe2\x80\x98<a href="/wiki/Feel_(Robbie_Williams_song)" title="Feel (Robbie Williams song)">Feel</a>,\xe2\x80\x99 were both exercises in melodic self loathing. It felt like a public airing of very private pain.\xe2\x80\x9d</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94<i>Robbie Williams, O2 London, review</i>, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" title="The Daily Telegraph">The Telegraph</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>Williams has reportedly battled <a href="/wiki/Mental_disorder" title="Mental disorder">mental illness</a>, <a href="/wiki/Obesity" title="Obesity">obesity</a>, <a href="/wiki/Self-esteem" title="Self-esteem">self-esteem</a> issues, <a href="/wiki/Alcoholism" title="Alcoholism">alcoholism</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Substance_abuse" title="Substance abuse">substance abuse</a> throughout his life.<sup id="cite_ref-heathfeel_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-heathfeel-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-independent.co.uk_129-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-independent.co.uk-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> He has discussed how his friend <a href="/wiki/Elton_John" title="Elton John">Elton John</a> booked him into a clinic to cope with his drug use that emerged from the <a href="/wiki/Major_depressive_disorder" title="Major depressive disorder">depression</a> he was experiencing while still in Take That.<sup id="cite_ref-independent.co.uk_129-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-independent.co.uk-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>He revealed in 2011 he had been battling <a href="/wiki/Lethargy" title="Lethargy">lethargy</a> caused by a type of <a href="/wiki/Hormone_imbalance" class="mw-redirect" title="Hormone imbalance">hormone imbalance</a> called <a href="/wiki/Andropause" class="mw-redirect" title="Andropause">andropause</a> for a number of years and thought at first it was a return of his depression.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interests">Interests</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Robbie_Williams,_Roundhouse,_London_(Apple_Music_Festival)_(29312808023).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Robbie_Williams%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival%29_%2829312808023%29.jpg/170px-Robbie_Williams%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival%29_%2829312808023%29.jpg" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Robbie_Williams%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival%29_%2829312808023%29.jpg/255px-Robbie_Williams%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival%29_%2829312808023%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Robbie_Williams%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival%29_%2829312808023%29.jpg/340px-Robbie_Williams%2C_Roundhouse%2C_London_%28Apple_Music_Festival%29_%2829312808023%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3456" data-file-height="4608" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Robbie_Williams,_Roundhouse,_London_(Apple_Music_Festival)_(29312808023).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>One of Williams\xe2\x80\x99 tattoos, the spectacles logo of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Two_Ronnies" title="The Two Ronnies">The Two Ronnies</a></i>, visible on his neck</div></div></div>\n<p>Williams has a strong interest in <a href="/wiki/UFO" class="mw-redirect" title="UFO">UFOs</a> and related <a href="/wiki/Paranormal" title="Paranormal">paranormal</a> phenomena, and has pursued this interest during his 2007\xe2\x80\x9308 sabbatical.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> His interest in the subject led to him taking part in a documentary for <a href="/wiki/BBC_Radio_4" title="BBC Radio 4">BBC Radio 4</a> with <a href="/wiki/Jon_Ronson" title="Jon Ronson">Jon Ronson</a>. The documentary followed them to a UFO convention in <a href="/wiki/Nevada" title="Nevada">Nevada</a> during which Williams connected his interest in the paranormal with the desire to understand his childhood fears of his mothers interest in "the world\'s mysteries, elves, demons, witchcraft".<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> Williams became an ordained minister with the <a href="/wiki/Universal_Life_Church_Monastery" title="Universal Life Church Monastery">Universal Life Church Monastery</a> to officiate the wedding of friends.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Williams has a number of body tattoos, most of which are related to British culture: image of an Ace of Spades\xe2\x80\x93commemorating heavy metal band <a href="/wiki/Mot%C3%B6rhead" title="Mot\xc3\xb6rhead">Mot\xc3\xb6rhead</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Fez" title="Fez">Fez</a>\xe2\x80\x93common headwear of comedian <a href="/wiki/Tommy_Cooper" title="Tommy Cooper">Tommy Cooper</a>, logo of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Saint_(TV_series)" title="The Saint (TV series)">The Saint</a></i>\xe2\x80\x93tribute to <a href="/wiki/Roger_Moore" title="Roger Moore">Roger Moore</a> who played the titular character on the TV show, spectacles logo of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Two_Ronnies" title="The Two Ronnies">The Two Ronnies</a></i>\xe2\x80\x93commemorating the comedy sketch show of the TV double act of <a href="/wiki/Ronnie_Barker" title="Ronnie Barker">Ronnie Barker</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronnie_Corbett" title="Ronnie Corbett">Ronnie Corbett</a>, image of the \xe2\x80\x9cskip dance\xe2\x80\x9d pose of <a href="/wiki/Morecambe_and_Wise" title="Morecambe and Wise">Morecambe and Wise</a>\xe2\x80\x93another TV comic double act <a href="/wiki/Eric_Morecambe" title="Eric Morecambe">Eric Morecambe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ernie_Wise" title="Ernie Wise">Ernie Wise</a>, image of a <a href="/wiki/Stafford_knot" title="Stafford knot">Staffordshire knot</a>\xe2\x80\x93Williams ancestors are from Staffordshire, logo of his former band <a href="/wiki/Take_That" title="Take That">Take That</a>, coat of arms of <a href="/wiki/Burslem" title="Burslem">Burslem</a>\xe2\x80\x93town in Stoke-on-Trent where Williams grew up, and the notes and words of the first line of the chorus of <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">the Beatles</a> song \xe2\x80\x9c<a href="/wiki/All_You_Need_Is_Love" title="All You Need Is Love">All You Need Is Love</a>\xe2\x80\x9d are tattooed on his lower back.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships_and_fatherhood">Relationships and fatherhood</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ayda_Field_Cannes_2015.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Ayda_Field_Cannes_2015.jpg/170px-Ayda_Field_Cannes_2015.jpg" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/0e/Ayda_Field_Cannes_2015.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="197" data-file-height="296" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ayda_Field_Cannes_2015.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Robbie Williams and Ayda Field (pictured) have been married since 2010</div></div></div>\n<p>Since May 2006, Williams has been in a relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Turkish_American" class="mw-redirect" title="Turkish American">American</a> actress <a href="/wiki/Ayda_Field" title="Ayda Field">Ayda Field</a>. She was featured in the UFO documentary that Williams did for BBC Radio 4 in April,<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> and took part in a field investigation he did in <a href="/wiki/Trout_Lake,_Washington" title="Trout Lake, Washington">Trout Lake, Washington</a> in August 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> There have been questions about Williams\'s sexuality, with some speculating that he may be <a href="/wiki/Bisexuality" title="Bisexuality">bisexual</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> In an interview with the <i>Daily Star</i>, he stated: "I love musical theatre and a lot of the other things that are often associated with gays. I am 49% homosexual and sometimes as far as 50%. However, that would imply that I enjoy having a particular sort of fun, which I don\'t."<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>On 26 November 2009, Williams proposed to Field live on the Australian radio channel <a href="/wiki/2DayFM" class="mw-redirect" title="2DayFM">2DayFM</a> in an interview on <i><a href="/wiki/The_Kyle_and_Jackie_O_Show" title="The Kyle and Jackie O Show">The Kyle and Jackie O Show</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> A few days later Williams denied the engagement, using his official blog to say "Hey all. We are not engaged. Rob."<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> Later it was confirmed that they became engaged over Christmas. She and Williams wed at his home in Mulholland Estates in <a href="/wiki/Beverly_Hills" class="mw-redirect" title="Beverly Hills">Beverly Hills</a> on 7 August 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Williams\' daughter Theodora "Teddy" Rose was born on 18 September 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> His second child Charlton "Charlie" Valentine was born on 27 October 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> His third child Colette \xe2\x80\x9cCoco\xe2\x80\x9d Josephine Williams was born on 7 September 2018 via surrogacy.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wealth">Wealth</span></h3>\n<p>In the 2011 <i><a href="/wiki/Sunday_Times_Rich_List" title="Sunday Times Rich List">Sunday Times Rich List</a></i> of wealthiest people in the British music industry, his wealth was estimated at \xc2\xa390&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> Williams is a lifelong supporter of football club <a href="/wiki/Port_Vale_F.C." title="Port Vale F.C.">Port Vale</a>, based in his home town of <a href="/wiki/Stoke-on-Trent" title="Stoke-on-Trent">Stoke-on-Trent</a>. In February 2006, he bought \xc2\xa3240,000 worth of shares in the club, making him the majority <a href="/wiki/Shareholder" title="Shareholder">shareholder</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> However the club entered <a href="/wiki/Administration_(British_football)" title="Administration (British football)">administration</a> on 9 March 2012, and as a result Williams lost all of his shares in the club and received only a fraction of his original investment back.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Charity">Charity</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg/170px-Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg" width="170" height="216" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg/255px-Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg/340px-Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg 2x" data-file-width="503" data-file-height="640" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Robbie_Williams_SoccerAid2006_Pre-Match_Training.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Williams warming up for the 2006 edition of <a href="/wiki/Soccer_Aid" title="Soccer Aid">Soccer Aid</a></div></div></div>\n<p>Williams has set up a charity in his home town of Stoke-on-Trent entitled <i>Give It Sum</i>, its goal being to "improve local conditions and strengthen community life by giving money to those who are disadvantaged."<sup id="cite_ref-heathfeel_128-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-heathfeel-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Williams, with the help of friend Jonathan Wilkes, has organised charity football matches called <a href="/wiki/Soccer_Aid" title="Soccer Aid">Soccer Aid</a> to raise money for <a href="/wiki/UNICEF_UK" title="UNICEF UK">UNICEF UK</a>. A mixture of celebrities and professional football players have played Soccer Aid matches in 2006, 2008, 2010, 2012, 2014, 2016 and 2018 at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a> in <a href="/wiki/Manchester" title="Manchester">Manchester</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Williams has been the Patron of the children\'s charity the Donna Louise Trust, based in Stoke-on-Trent, since 2002. The charity offers respite and palliative care to <a href="/wiki/Terminal_illness" title="Terminal illness">terminally ill</a> and life-limited children who are not expected to live past the age of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Awards_and_nominations">Awards and nominations</span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Robbie_Williams" title="List of awards and nominations received by Robbie Williams">List of awards and nominations received by Robbie Williams</a></div>\n<p>Williams has won various awards with some of his more recognised accolades being the <a href="/wiki/Brit_Awards" title="Brit Awards">Brit Awards</a>. He has won a record eighteen Brit Awards which also include the Brits he won with <a href="/wiki/Take_That" title="Take That">Take That</a> making him the most successful artist in the history of the awards.<sup id="cite_ref-Brits_Icon_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Brits_Icon-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> He has also won 8 Echo Awards from the German music industry.<sup id="cite_ref-rhein-zeitung.de_116-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rhein-zeitung.de-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Discography">Discography</span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Robbie_Williams_discography" title="Robbie Williams discography">Robbie Williams discography</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_songs_recorded_by_Robbie_Williams" title="List of songs recorded by Robbie Williams">List of songs recorded by Robbie Williams</a></div>\n<dl><dt>Studio albums</dt></dl>\n<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Life_thru_a_Lens" title="Life thru a Lens">Life thru a You&#39;re Winning">Swing When You\'re Winning</a></i> (2001)</li>\n<li><i><a href="/wiki/Escapology_(album)" title="Escapology (album)">Escapology</a></i> (2002)</li>\n<li><i><a
